                    [32m'var GET_SKILL_FETCH_TIMEOUT_MS = 5000;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'var LANGFUSE_FLAGS = new Set([\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  "--public-key",\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  "--secret-key",\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  "--host",\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  "--env"\n'[39m +
                    [32m']);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'var LANGFUSE_BOOL_FLAGS = new Set(["--refetch-api-spec"]);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function loadEnvFile(filePath) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const content = readFileSync(filePath, "utf-8");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  for (const line of content.split(`\n'[39m +
                    [32m'`)) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const trimmed = line.trim();\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    if (!trimmed || trimmed.startsWith("#"))\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      continue;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const eqIdx = trimmed.indexOf("=");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    if (eqIdx === -1)\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      continue;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const key = trimmed.slice(0, eqIdx).trim();\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    let val = trimmed.slice(eqIdx + 1).trim();\n'[39m +
                    [32m`    if (val.startsWith('"') && val.endsWith('"') || val.startsWith("'") && val.endsWith("'")) {\n`[39m +
                    [32m'      val = val.slice(1, -1);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    process.env[key] = val;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'async function loadMain() {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const specliEntry = import.meta.resolve("specli");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const cliMainUrl = new URL("cli/main.js", specliEntry);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const mod = await import(cliMainUrl.href);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return mod.main;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'async function getSpecText(params) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (params.refetch) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const specUrl = `${params.host}/generated/api/openapi.yml`;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return fetchText(specUrl, "spec");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return readFileSync(OPENAPI_FILE_URL, "utf-8");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'async function fetchText(url, label, options) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const resp = await fetch(url, {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    signal: typeof options?.timeoutMs === "number" ? AbortSignal.timeout(options.timeoutMs) : undefined\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (!resp.ok) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    throw new Error(`Failed to fetch ${label} from ${url}: ${resp.status} ${resp.statusText}`);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return resp.text();\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'async function getSkillText() {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return fetchText(LANGFUSE_SKILL_URL, "skill", {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    timeoutMs: GET_SKILL_FETCH_TIMEOUT_MS\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function printGetSkillFetchError(err) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const reason = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  process.stderr.write(`Failed to fetch the latest Langfuse skill from GitHub.\n'[39m +
                    [32m'This environment may block direct GitHub access.\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Download the skill manually from:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  ${LANGFUSE_SKILL_URL}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Then add the downloaded SKILL.md to your agent context manually.\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Original error: ${reason}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'`);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'async function run(argv) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const extracted = {};\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const boolFlags = {};\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const passthrough = [argv[0], argv[1]];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  let i = 2;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  while (i < argv.length) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    if (LANGFUSE_FLAGS.has(argv[i]) && i + 1 < argv.length) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      const key = argv[i].replace(/^--/, "");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      extracted[key] = argv[i + 1];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      i += 2;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    } else if (LANGFUSE_BOOL_FLAGS.has(argv[i])) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      const key = argv[i].replace(/^--/, "");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      boolFlags[key] = true;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      i++;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    } else {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      passthrough.push(argv[i]);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      i++;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (extracted["env"]) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    loadEnvFile(extracted["env"]);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const publicKey = extracted["public-key"] ?? process.env.LANGFUSE_PUBLIC_KEY;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const secretKey = extracted["secret-key"] ?? process.env.LANGFUSE_SECRET_KEY;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const host = (extracted["host"] ?? process.env.LANGFUSE_BASE_URL ?? process.env.LANGFUSE_HOST ?? DEFAULT_HOST).replace(/\\/$/, "");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const subcommand = passthrough[2];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (subcommand === "api") {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    passthrough.splice(2, 1);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return runApi({ passthrough, boolFlags, publicKey, secretKey, host });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (subcommand === "get-skill") {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    try {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      process.stdout.write(await getSkillText());\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    } catch (err) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      printGetSkillFetchError(err);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      process.exitCode = 1;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  printHelp();\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function printHelp() {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  console.log(`langfuse-cli — Interact with Langfuse from the command line\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Usage: langfuse [options] <command>\n'[39m +

                    [32m'  api                     Interact with the Langfuse REST API\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  get-skill               Print the latest Langfuse skill from GitHub\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Options:\n'[39m +

                    [32m'  --secret-key <key>      Langfuse secret key (or LANGFUSE_SECRET_KEY)\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --host <url>            Langfuse host (or LANGFUSE_HOST/LANGFUSE_BASE_URL, default: ${DEFAULT_HOST})\n'[39m +

            [32m'2. Non-trivial and complex tasks - Tasks that require careful planning or multiple operations\n'[39m +
            [32m'3. User explicitly requests todo list - When the user directly asks you to use the todo list\n'[39m +
            [32m'4. User provides multiple tasks - When users provide a list of things to be done (numbered or comma-separated)\n'[39m +
            [32m'5. After receiving new instructions - Immediately capture user requirements as todos. Feel free to edit the todo list based on new information.\n'[39m +
            [32m'6. After completing a task - Mark it complete and add any new follow-up tasks\n'[39m +
            [32m'7. When you start working on a new task, mark the todo as in-progress. Ideally you should only have one todo as in-progress at a time. Complete existing tasks before starting new ones.\n'[39m +

                value: {
                  content: [32m'// src/cli.ts\n'[39m +
                    [32m'import { readFileSync } from "node:fs";\n'[39m +
                    [32m'var DEFAULT_HOST = "https://cloud.langfuse.com";\n'[39m +
                    [32m'var OPENAPI_FILE_URL = new URL("../openapi.yml", import.meta.url);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'var LANGFUSE_SKILL_URL = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/langfuse/skills/main/skills/langfuse/SKILL.md";\n'[39m +
                    [32m'var GET_SKILL_FETCH_TIMEOUT_MS = 5000;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'var LANGFUSE_FLAGS = new Set([\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  "--public-key",\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  "--secret-key",\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  "--host",\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  "--env"\n'[39m +
                    [32m']);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'var LANGFUSE_BOOL_FLAGS = new Set(["--refetch-api-spec"]);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function loadEnvFile(filePath) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const content = readFileSync(filePath, "utf-8");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  for (const line of content.split(`\n'[39m +
                    [32m'`)) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const trimmed = line.trim();\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    if (!trimmed || trimmed.startsWith("#"))\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      continue;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const eqIdx = trimmed.indexOf("=");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    if (eqIdx === -1)\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      continue;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const key = trimmed.slice(0, eqIdx).trim();\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    let val = trimmed.slice(eqIdx + 1).trim();\n'[39m +
                    [32m`    if (val.startsWith('"') && val.endsWith('"') || val.startsWith("'") && val.endsWith("'")) {\n`[39m +
                    [32m'      val = val.slice(1, -1);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    process.env[key] = val;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'async function loadMain() {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const specliEntry = import.meta.resolve("specli");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const cliMainUrl = new URL("cli/main.js", specliEntry);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const mod = await import(cliMainUrl.href);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return mod.main;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'async function getSpecText(params) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (params.refetch) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const specUrl = `${params.host}/generated/api/openapi.yml`;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return fetchText(specUrl, "spec");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return readFileSync(OPENAPI_FILE_URL, "utf-8");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'async function fetchText(url, label, options) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const resp = await fetch(url, {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    signal: typeof options?.timeoutMs === "number" ? AbortSignal.timeout(options.timeoutMs) : undefined\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (!resp.ok) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    throw new Error(`Failed to fetch ${label} from ${url}: ${resp.status} ${resp.statusText}`);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +

                    [32m'}\n'[39m +

                    [32m'}\n'[39m +

                    [32m'  const reason = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  process.stderr.write(`Failed to fetch the latest Langfuse skill from GitHub.\n'[39m +
                    [32m'This environment may block direct GitHub access.\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Download the skill manually from:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  ${LANGFUSE_SKILL_URL}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Then add the downloaded SKILL.md to your agent context manually.\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Original error: ${reason}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'`);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'async function run(argv) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const extracted = {};\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const boolFlags = {};\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const passthrough = [argv[0], argv[1]];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  let i = 2;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  while (i < argv.length) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    if (LANGFUSE_FLAGS.has(argv[i]) && i + 1 < argv.length) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      const key = argv[i].replace(/^--/, "");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      extracted[key] = argv[i + 1];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      i += 2;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    } else if (LANGFUSE_BOOL_FLAGS.has(argv[i])) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      const key = argv[i].replace(/^--/, "");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      boolFlags[key] = true;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      i++;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    } else {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      passthrough.push(argv[i]);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      i++;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (extracted["env"]) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    loadEnvFile(extracted["env"]);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const publicKey = extracted["public-key"] ?? process.env.LANGFUSE_PUBLIC_KEY;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const secretKey = extracted["secret-key"] ?? process.env.LANGFUSE_SECRET_KEY;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const host = (extracted["host"] ?? process.env.LANGFUSE_BASE_URL ?? process.env.LANGFUSE_HOST ?? DEFAULT_HOST).replace(/\\/$/, "");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const subcommand = passthrough[2];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (subcommand === "api") {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    passthrough.splice(2, 1);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return runApi({ passthrough, boolFlags, publicKey, secretKey, host });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (subcommand === "get-skill") {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    try {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      process.stdout.write(await getSkillText());\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    } catch (err) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      printGetSkillFetchError(err);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      process.exitCode = 1;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  printHelp();\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function printHelp() {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  console.log(`langfuse-cli — Interact with Langfuse from the command line\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Usage: langfuse [options] <command>\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Commands:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  api                     Interact with the Langfuse REST API\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  get-skill               Print the latest Langfuse skill from GitHub\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Options:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --public-key <key>      Langfuse public key (or LANGFUSE_PUBLIC_KEY)\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --secret-key <key>      Langfuse secret key (or LANGFUSE_SECRET_KEY)\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --host <url>            Langfuse host (or LANGFUSE_HOST/LANGFUSE_BASE_URL, default: ${DEFAULT_HOST})\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --env <path>       Load env vars from file\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --refetch-api-spec      Fetch latest API spec instead of bundled\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Examples:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  langfuse api __schema                              List all available resources\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  langfuse api <resource> --help                     Show actions for a resource\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  langfuse api traces list --limit 10                List traces\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  langfuse api prompts list                          List prompts\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  langfuse api scores create --name quality \\\\\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    --traceId <id> --value 0.9                       Create a score\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  langfuse api datasets create --name my-dataset     Create a dataset`);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function printApiHelp(resources) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const sorted = [...resources].sort();\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  console.log(`Usage: langfuse api [options] <resource> <action>\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Langfuse API Resources:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'${sorted.map((r) => `  ${r}`).join(`\n'[39m +
                    [32m'`)}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Commands:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  __schema                Show API spec metadata\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  <resource> --help       Show actions for a resource\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  <resource> <action> --help  Show options for an action\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Options:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --json                  Output as JSON\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --curl                  Preview curl command without executing\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  -h, --help              Show help\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Workflow:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  1) langfuse api __schema\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  2) langfuse api <resource> --help\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  3) langfuse api <resource> <action> --help\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  4) langfuse api <resource> <action> [options]`);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'async function getResources(specText) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const main = await loadMain();\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const chunks = [];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const origWrite = process.stdout.write.bind(process.stdout);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  process.stdout.write = (chunk) => {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    chunks.push(String(chunk));\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return true;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  };\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  try {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    await main(["node", "langfuse", "__schema", "--json"], {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      cliName: "langfuse api",\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      auth: "BasicAuth",\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      embeddedSpecText: specText\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  } finally {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    process.stdout.write = origWrite;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const output = JSON.parse(chunks.join(""));\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return (output.data?.resources ?? []).map((r) => r.name);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'async function runApi(params) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const { passthrough, boolFlags, publicKey, secretKey, host } = params;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const specText = await getSpecText({\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    refetch: boolFlags["refetch-api-spec"] ?? false,\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    host\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const args = passthrough.slice(2);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (args.length === 0 || args.length === 1 && (args[0] === "--help" || args[0] === "-h")) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    printApiHelp(await getResources(specText));\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const specliArgv = [...passthrough];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const inject = ["--server", host];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (publicKey)\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    inject.push("--username", publicKey);\n'[39m +

                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### exec\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Run commands dynamically from any OpenAPI spec URL or file path. Works with both Node.js and Bun.\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```bash\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli exec <spec> <resource> <action> [args...] [options]\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'**Examples:**\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```bash\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Inspect available commands\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli exec ./openapi.json __schema\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Machine-readable schema output\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli exec ./openapi.json __schema --json\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Minimal schema (best for large specs)\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli exec ./openapi.json __schema --json --min\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Run an operation\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli exec ./openapi.json users list\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Run with path parameters\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli exec ./openapi.json users get abc123\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Preview the curl command without executing\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli exec ./openapi.json users list --curl\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Dry run (show request details without executing)\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli exec ./openapi.json users list --dry-run\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### compile\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Bundle an OpenAPI spec into a standalone executable. **Requires Bun.**\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```bash\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli compile <spec> [options]\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'**Options:**\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| Option | Description |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'|--------|-------------|\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--name <name>` | Binary name (default: derived from spec title) |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--outfile <path>` | Output path (default: `./out/<name>`) |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--target <target>` | Cross-compile target (e.g. `bun-linux-x64`) |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--minify` | Enable minification |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--bytecode` | Enable bytecode compilation |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--no-dotenv` | Disable .env autoload |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--no-bunfig` | Disable bunfig.toml autoload |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--server <url>` | Bake in a default server URL |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--server-var <k=v>` | Bake in server variables (repeatable) |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--auth <scheme>` | Bake in default auth scheme |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'**Examples:**\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```bash\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Compile with auto-derived name\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli compile ./openapi.yaml\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Creates: ./out/my-api\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Compile with explicit name\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli compile ./openapi.yaml --name myapi\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Creates: ./out/myapi\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Cross-compile for Linux\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli compile ./openapi.json --target bun-linux-x64 --outfile ./out/myapi-linux\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Bake in defaults\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli compile https://api.example.com/openapi.json \\\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --name myapi \\\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --server https://api.example.com \\\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --auth BearerAuth\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'The compiled binary works standalone:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```bash\n'[39m +
                    [32m'./dist/myapi users list\n'[39m +
                    [32m'./dist/myapi users get abc123 --json\n'[39m +

                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## CLI Shape\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli generates commands of the form:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\n'[39m +
                    [32m'<resource> <action> [...positionals] [options]\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- **resource**: Derived from `tags[0]`, `operationId` prefix, or first path segment\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- **action**: Inferred from HTTP method or `operationId` suffix\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- Name collisions are disambiguated automatically\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Use `__schema` to see the command mapping for any spec.\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Global Options\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| Option | Description |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'|--------|-------------|\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--server <url>` | Override server/base URL |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--server-var <name=value>` | Server URL template variable (repeatable) |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--profile <name>` | Profile name |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--auth <scheme>` | Select auth scheme by key |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--bearer-token <token>` | Set `Authorization: Bearer <token>` |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--oauth-token <token>` | Alias for `--bearer-token` |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--username <user>` | Basic auth username |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--password <pass>` | Basic auth password |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--api-key <key>` | API key value |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--json` | Machine-readable output |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Per-Operation Options\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Every operation command includes:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| Option | Description |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'|--------|-------------|\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--header <header>` | Extra headers (repeatable, `Name: Value` or `Name=Value`) |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--accept <type>` | Override `Accept` header |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--timeout <ms>` | Request timeout in milliseconds |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--dry-run` | Print request details without sending |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--curl` | Print equivalent curl command without sending |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'For operations with request bodies:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| Option | Description |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'|--------|-------------|\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--data <data>` | Inline request body |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--file <path>` | Read request body from file |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--content-type <type>` | Override `Content-Type` |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Parameters\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### Path Parameters\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Path parameters become positional arguments in order:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\n'[39m +
                    [32m'/users/{id}/keys/{key_id}  →  <id> <key-id>\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### Query/Header/Cookie Parameters\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'These become kebab-case flags:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\n'[39m +
                    [32m'limit        → --limit\n'[39m +
                    [32m'X-Request-Id → --x-request-id\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Required parameters are enforced by the CLI.\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### Arrays\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Array parameters are repeatable:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```bash\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# All produce ?tag=a&tag=b\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli ... --tag a --tag b\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli ... --tag a,b\n'[39m +
                    [32m`specli ... --tag '["a","b"]'\n`[39m +
                    [32m'```\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Request Bodies\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +

                    [32m'## Programmatic API\n'[39m +

                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function collectFlags(properties, pathPrefix, requiredAtRoot, out, reservedFlags) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    for (const [name, propSchema] of Object.entries(properties)) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        if (!name || typeof name !== "string")\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            continue;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        if (!propSchema || typeof propSchema !== "object")\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            continue;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        const path = [...pathPrefix, name];\n'[39m +

                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return result;\n'[39m +

                    [32m'/**\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * Set a value at a nested path, creating intermediate objects as needed.\n'[39m +

                    [32m'function setNestedValue(obj, path, value, type) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    let current = obj;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    for (let i = 0; i < path.length - 1; i++) {\n'[39m +

                    [32m'            current[key] = {};\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        current = current[key];\n'[39m +

                    [32m'        current[finalKey] = true;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +

                    [32m'        current[finalKey] = Number.parseInt(String(value), 10);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    else if (type === "number") {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        current[finalKey] = Number(String(value));\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    else {\n'[39m +

                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return missing;\n'[39m +

                    [32m'function formatCustomHelp(cmd, action, operationFlags, bodyFlagDefs) {\n'[39m +

                    [32m'    lines.push("  -h, --help\\n      Show this help message");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    lines.push("");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return lines.join("\\n");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'export function addGeneratedCommands(program, context) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    for (const resource of context.commands.resources) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        const resourceCmd = program\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            .command(resource.resource)\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            .description(`Operations for ${resource.resource}`);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        for (const action of resource.actions) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            const cmd = resourceCmd.command(action.action);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            cmd.description(action.summary ??\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                action.description ??\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                `${action.method} ${action.path}`);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            for (const pos of action.positionals) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                cmd.argument(`<${pos.name}>`, pos.description);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            for (const flag of action.flags) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                const opt = flag.flag;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                const desc = flag.description ?? `${flag.in} parameter`;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                if (flag.type === "boolean") {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                    cmd.option(opt, desc);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                    continue;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                const isArray = flag.type === "array";\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                const itemType = flag.itemType ?? "string";\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                const flagType = isArray ? itemType : flag.type;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                const parser = (raw) => coerceValue(raw, flagType);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                if (isArray) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                    const key = `${opt} <value>`;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                    cmd.option(key, desc, (value, prev) => {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                        const next = [...(prev ?? [])];\n'[39m +

                    [32m'  "--secret-key",\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  "--host",\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  "--env"\n'[39m +
                    [32m']);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'var LANGFUSE_BOOL_FLAGS = new Set(["--refetch-api-spec"]);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function loadEnvFile(filePath) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const content = readFileSync(filePath, "utf-8");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  for (const line of content.split(`\n'[39m +
                    [32m'`)) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const trimmed = line.trim();\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    if (!trimmed || trimmed.startsWith("#"))\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      continue;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const eqIdx = trimmed.indexOf("=");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    if (eqIdx === -1)\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      continue;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const key = trimmed.slice(0, eqIdx).trim();\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    let val = trimmed.slice(eqIdx + 1).trim();\n'[39m +
                    [32m`    if (val.startsWith('"') && val.endsWith('"') || val.startsWith("'") && val.endsWith("'")) {\n`[39m +
                    [32m'      val = val.slice(1, -1);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    process.env[key] = val;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'async function loadMain() {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const specliEntry = import.meta.resolve("specli");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const cliMainUrl = new URL("cli/main.js", specliEntry);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const mod = await import(cliMainUrl.href);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return mod.main;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'async function getSpecText(params) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (params.refetch) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const specUrl = `${params.host}/generated/api/openapi.yml`;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return fetchText(specUrl, "spec");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return readFileSync(OPENAPI_FILE_URL, "utf-8");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'async function fetchText(url, label, options) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const resp = await fetch(url, {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    signal: typeof options?.timeoutMs === "number" ? AbortSignal.timeout(options.timeoutMs) : undefined\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (!resp.ok) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    throw new Error(`Failed to fetch ${label} from ${url}: ${resp.status} ${resp.statusText}`);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return resp.text();\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'async function getSkillText() {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return fetchText(LANGFUSE_SKILL_URL, "skill", {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    timeoutMs: GET_SKILL_FETCH_TIMEOUT_MS\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function printGetSkillFetchError(err) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const reason = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  process.stderr.write(`Failed to fetch the latest Langfuse skill from GitHub.\n'[39m +
                    [32m'This environment may block direct GitHub access.\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Download the skill manually from:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  ${LANGFUSE_SKILL_URL}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Then add the downloaded SKILL.md to your agent context manually.\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Original error: ${reason}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'`);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'async function run(argv) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const extracted = {};\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const boolFlags = {};\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const passthrough = [argv[0], argv[1]];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  let i = 2;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  while (i < argv.length) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    if (LANGFUSE_FLAGS.has(argv[i]) && i + 1 < argv.length) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      const key = argv[i].replace(/^--/, "");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      extracted[key] = argv[i + 1];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      i += 2;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    } else if (LANGFUSE_BOOL_FLAGS.has(argv[i])) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      const key = argv[i].replace(/^--/, "");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      boolFlags[key] = true;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      i++;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    } else {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      passthrough.push(argv[i]);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      i++;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (extracted["env"]) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    loadEnvFile(extracted["env"]);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const publicKey = extracted["public-key"] ?? process.env.LANGFUSE_PUBLIC_KEY;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const secretKey = extracted["secret-key"] ?? process.env.LANGFUSE_SECRET_KEY;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const host = (extracted["host"] ?? process.env.LANGFUSE_BASE_URL ?? process.env.LANGFUSE_HOST ?? DEFAULT_HOST).replace(/\\/$/, "");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const subcommand = passthrough[2];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (subcommand === "api") {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    passthrough.splice(2, 1);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return runApi({ passthrough, boolFlags, publicKey, secretKey, host });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (subcommand === "get-skill") {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    try {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      process.stdout.write(await getSkillText());\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    } catch (err) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      printGetSkillFetchError(err);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      process.exitCode = 1;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  printHelp();\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function printHelp() {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  console.log(`langfuse-cli — Interact with Langfuse from the command line\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Usage: langfuse [options] <command>\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Commands:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  api                     Interact with the Langfuse REST API\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  get-skill               Print the latest Langfuse skill from GitHub\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Options:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --public-key <key>      Langfuse public key (or LANGFUSE_PUBLIC_KEY)\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --secret-key <key>      Langfuse secret key (or LANGFUSE_SECRET_KEY)\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --host <url>            Langfuse host (or LANGFUSE_HOST/LANGFUSE_BASE_URL, default: ${DEFAULT_HOST})\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --env <path>       Load env vars from file\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --refetch-api-spec      Fetch latest API spec instead of bundled\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Examples:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  langfuse api __schema                              List all available resources\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  langfuse api <resource> --help                     Show actions for a resource\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  langfuse api traces list --limit 10                List traces\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  langfuse api prompts list                          List prompts\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  langfuse api scores create --name quality \\\\\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    --traceId <id> --value 0.9                       Create a score\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  langfuse api datasets create --name my-dataset     Create a dataset`);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function printApiHelp(resources) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const sorted = [...resources].sort();\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  console.log(`Usage: langfuse api [options] <resource> <action>\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Langfuse API Resources:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'${sorted.map((r) => `  ${r}`).join(`\n'[39m +
                    [32m'`)}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Commands:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  __schema                Show API spec metadata\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  <resource> --help       Show actions for a resource\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  <resource> <action> --help  Show options for an action\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Options:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --json                  Output as JSON\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --curl                  Preview curl command without executing\n'[39m +

                    [32m'  3) langfuse api <resource> <action> --help\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  4) langfuse api <resource> <action> [options]`);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'async function getResources(specText) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const main = await loadMain();\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const chunks = [];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const origWrite = process.stdout.write.bind(process.stdout);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  process.stdout.write = (chunk) => {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    chunks.push(String(chunk));\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return true;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  };\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  try {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    await main(["node", "langfuse", "__schema", "--json"], {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      cliName: "langfuse api",\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      auth: "BasicAuth",\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      embeddedSpecText: specText\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  } finally {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    process.stdout.write = origWrite;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const output = JSON.parse(chunks.join(""));\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return (output.data?.resources ?? []).map((r) => r.name);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'async function runApi(params) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const { passthrough, boolFlags, publicKey, secretKey, host } = params;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const specText = await getSpecText({\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    refetch: boolFlags["refetch-api-spec"] ?? false,\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    host\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const args = passthrough.slice(2);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (args.length === 0 || args.length === 1 && (args[0] === "--help" || args[0] === "-h")) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    printApiHelp(await getResources(specText));\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const specliArgv = [...passthrough];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const inject = ["--server", host];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (publicKey)\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    inject.push("--username", publicKey);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (secretKey)\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    inject.push("--password", secretKey);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  specliArgv.splice(2, 0, ...inject);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const main = await loadMain();\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  await main(specliArgv, {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    cliName: "langfuse api",\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    auth: "BasicAuth",\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    embeddedSpecText: specText\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'export {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  run\n'[39m +
                    [32m'};\n'[39m +

                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### exec\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Run commands dynamically from any OpenAPI spec URL or file path. Works with both Node.js and Bun.\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```bash\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli exec <spec> <resource> <action> [args...] [options]\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'**Examples:**\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```bash\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Inspect available commands\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli exec ./openapi.json __schema\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Machine-readable schema output\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli exec ./openapi.json __schema --json\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Minimal schema (best for large specs)\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli exec ./openapi.json __schema --json --min\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Run an operation\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli exec ./openapi.json users list\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Run with path parameters\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli exec ./openapi.json users get abc123\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Preview the curl command without executing\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli exec ./openapi.json users list --curl\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Dry run (show request details without executing)\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli exec ./openapi.json users list --dry-run\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### compile\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Bundle an OpenAPI spec into a standalone executable. **Requires Bun.**\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```bash\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli compile <spec> [options]\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'**Options:**\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| Option | Description |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'|--------|-------------|\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--name <name>` | Binary name (default: derived from spec title) |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--outfile <path>` | Output path (default: `./out/<name>`) |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--target <target>` | Cross-compile target (e.g. `bun-linux-x64`) |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--minify` | Enable minification |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--bytecode` | Enable bytecode compilation |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--no-dotenv` | Disable .env autoload |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--no-bunfig` | Disable bunfig.toml autoload |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--server <url>` | Bake in a default server URL |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--server-var <k=v>` | Bake in server variables (repeatable) |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--auth <scheme>` | Bake in default auth scheme |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'**Examples:**\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```bash\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Compile with auto-derived name\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli compile ./openapi.yaml\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Creates: ./out/my-api\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Compile with explicit name\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli compile ./openapi.yaml --name myapi\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Creates: ./out/myapi\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Cross-compile for Linux\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli compile ./openapi.json --target bun-linux-x64 --outfile ./out/myapi-linux\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Bake in defaults\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli compile https://api.example.com/openapi.json \\\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --name myapi \\\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --server https://api.example.com \\\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  --auth BearerAuth\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'The compiled binary works standalone:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```bash\n'[39m +
                    [32m'./dist/myapi users list\n'[39m +
                    [32m'./dist/myapi users get abc123 --json\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## CLI Shape\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'specli generates commands of the form:\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\n'[39m +
                    [32m'<resource> <action> [...positionals] [options]\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- **resource**: Derived from `tags[0]`, `operationId` prefix, or first path segment\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- **action**: Inferred from HTTP method or `operationId` suffix\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- Name collisions are disambiguated automatically\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Use `__schema` to see the command mapping for any spec.\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Global Options\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| Option | Description |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'|--------|-------------|\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--server <url>` | Override server/base URL |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--server-var <name=value>` | Server URL template variable (repeatable) |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--profile <name>` | Profile name |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--auth <scheme>` | Select auth scheme by key |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--bearer-token <token>` | Set `Authorization: Bearer <token>` |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--oauth-token <token>` | Alias for `--bearer-token` |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--username <user>` | Basic auth username |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--password <pass>` | Basic auth password |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--api-key <key>` | API key value |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--json` | Machine-readable output |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Per-Operation Options\n'[39m +

                    [32m'| Option | Description |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'|--------|-------------|\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--header <header>` | Extra headers (repeatable, `Name: Value` or `Name=Value`) |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--accept <type>` | Override `Accept` header |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--timeout <ms>` | Request timeout in milliseconds |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--dry-run` | Print request details without sending |\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| `--curl` | Print equivalent curl command without sending |\n'[39m +

                value: {
                  content: [32m'/**\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * Body flag generation and parsing utilities.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * Generates CLI flags from JSON schema properties and parses\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * dot-notation flags back into nested objects.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' */\n'[39m +
                    [32m'/**\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * Generate flag definitions from a JSON schema.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * Recursively handles nested objects using dot notation.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' */\n'[39m +
                    [32m'export function generateBodyFlags(schema, reservedFlags) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    if (!schema || schema.type !== "object" || !schema.properties) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        return [];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const flags = [];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const requiredSet = new Set(schema.required ?? []);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    collectFlags(schema.properties, [], requiredSet, flags, reservedFlags);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return flags;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function collectFlags(properties, pathPrefix, requiredAtRoot, out, reservedFlags) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    for (const [name, propSchema] of Object.entries(properties)) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        if (!name || typeof name !== "string")\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            continue;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        if (!propSchema || typeof propSchema !== "object")\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            continue;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        const path = [...pathPrefix, name];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        const flagName = `--${path.join(".")}`;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        // Skip if this flag would conflict with an operation parameter\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        if (reservedFlags.has(flagName))\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            continue;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        const t = propSchema.type;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        if (t === "object" && propSchema.properties) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            // Recurse into nested object\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            const nestedRequired = new Set(propSchema.required ?? []);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            collectFlags(propSchema.properties, path, nestedRequired, out, reservedFlags);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        else if (t === "string" ||\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            t === "number" ||\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            t === "integer" ||\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            t === "boolean") {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            // Leaf property - generate a flag\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            const isRequired = pathPrefix.length === 0 ? requiredAtRoot.has(name) : false;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            out.push({\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                flag: flagName,\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                path,\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                type: t,\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                description: propSchema.description ?? `Body field \'${path.join(".")}\'`,\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                required: isRequired,\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        // Skip arrays and other complex types for now\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'/**\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * Parse flag values with dot notation into a nested object.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * Example:\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *   { "address.street": "123 Main", "address.city": "NYC", "name": "Ada" }\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * Becomes:\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *   { address: { street: "123 Main", city: "NYC" }, name: "Ada" }\n'[39m +
                    [32m' */\n'[39m +
                    [32m'export function parseDotNotationFlags(flagValues, flagDefs) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const result = {};\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    for (const def of flagDefs) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        // Commander keeps dots in option names: --address.street -> "address.street"\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        const dotKey = def.path.join(".");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        const value = flagValues[dotKey];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        if (value === undefined)\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            continue;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        setNestedValue(result, def.path, value, def.type);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return result;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'/**\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * Set a value at a nested path, creating intermediate objects as needed.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' */\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function setNestedValue(obj, path, value, type) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    let current = obj;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    for (let i = 0; i < path.length - 1; i++) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        const key = path[i];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        if (!(key in current) || typeof current[key] !== "object") {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            current[key] = {};\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        current = current[key];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const finalKey = path[path.length - 1];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    // Coerce value based on type\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    if (type === "boolean") {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        current[finalKey] = true;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    else if (type === "integer") {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        current[finalKey] = Number.parseInt(String(value), 10);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    else if (type === "number") {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        current[finalKey] = Number(String(value));\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    else {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        current[finalKey] = String(value);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +

                    [32m'        }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return missing;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +

                    [32m'                throw new Error("Body field flags are only supported for JSON request bodies.");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            // Check for missing required fields\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            const { findMissingRequired, parseDotNotationFlags } = await import("./body-flags.js");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            const missing = findMissingRequired(input.flagValues, bodyFlagDefs);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            if (missing.length > 0) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                const missingFlags = missing.map((m) => `--${m}`).join(", ");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                throw new Error(`Missing required fields: ${missingFlags}`);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            // Build nested object from dot-notation flags\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            const built = parseDotNotationFlags(input.flagValues, bodyFlagDefs);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            if (schema) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                const validate = ajv.compile(schema);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                if (!validate(built)) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                    throw new Error(formatAjvErrors(validate.errors));\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            body = JSON.stringify(built);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    // Check if user has a stored token (needed for auth scheme auto-selection)\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const storedToken = profile?.name\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        ? await getToken(input.specId, profile.name)\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        : null;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    // Auth resolution priority: CLI flag > profile > embedded default\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const resolvedAuthScheme = resolveAuthScheme(input.authSchemes, input.action.auth, {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        flagAuthScheme: input.globals.auth,\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        profileAuthScheme: profile?.authScheme,\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        embeddedAuthScheme: embedded?.auth,\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        hasStoredToken: Boolean(storedToken),\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const tokenFromProfile = resolvedAuthScheme ? storedToken : null;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const globalsWithProfileAuth = {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        ...input.globals,\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        auth: resolvedAuthScheme,\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        bearerToken: input.globals.bearerToken ??\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            input.globals.oauthToken ??\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            tokenFromProfile ??\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            undefined,\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    };\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const final = applyAuth(headers, url, input.action, globalsWithProfileAuth, input.authSchemes);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const req = new Request(final.url.toString(), {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        method: input.action.method,\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        headers: final.headers,\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        body,\n'[39m +

                    [32m'    return { request: req, curl, body };\n'[39m +

                    [32m'function buildCurl(req, body) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const parts = ["curl", "-sS", "-X", req.method];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    for (const [k, v] of req.headers.entries()) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        const value = k.toLowerCase() === "authorization" ? maskAuthHeader(v) : v;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        parts.push("-H", shellQuote(`${k}: ${value}`));\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +

                    [32m'        parts.push("--data", shellQuote(body));\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    parts.push(shellQuote(req.url));\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return parts.join(" ");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function maskAuthHeader(value) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    // Mask token in authorization header, preserving scheme (e.g., "Bearer")\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    // "Bearer abc123xyz" -> "Bearer abc...xyz"\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const parts = value.split(" ");\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    if (parts.length === 2) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        const [scheme, token] = parts;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        return `${scheme} ${maskToken(token)}`;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    // No scheme, just mask the whole value\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return maskToken(value);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function maskToken(token) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    if (token.length <= 6) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        return "***";\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const prefix = token.slice(0, 3);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const suffix = token.slice(-3);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return `${prefix}...${suffix}`;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function shellQuote(value) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m"    return `'${value.replace(/'/g, `'\\\\''`)}'`;\n"[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function optionKeyFromFlag(flag) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    // Commander uses camelCase property names derived from long flag.\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    // Example: --x-request-id -> xRequestId\n'[39m +

                    [32m'    return name.replace(/-([a-z])/g, (_, c) => String(c).toUpperCase());\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m''[39m,
                  isTruncated: [33mfalse[39m
                }

            [32m'     - python /path/with spaces/script.py (incorrect - will fail)\n'[39m +

            [32m'   - Capture the output of the command.\n'[39m +

            [32m'# Committing changes with git\n'[39m +
            [32m'\n'[39m +
            [32m'Only create commits when requested by the user. If unclear, ask first. When the user asks you to create a new git commit, follow these steps carefully:\n'[39m +
            [32m'\n'[39m +
            [32m'Git Safety Protocol:\n'[39m +
            [32m'- NEVER update the git config\n'[39m +
            [32m"- NEVER run destructive git commands (push --force, reset --hard, checkout ., restore ., clean -f, branch -D) unless the user explicitly requests these actions. Taking unauthorized destructive actions is unhelpful and can result in lost work, so it's best to ONLY run these commands when given direct instructions \n"[39m +
            [32m'- NEVER skip hooks (--no-verify, --no-gpg-sign, etc) unless the user explicitly requests it\n'[39m +
            [32m'- NEVER run force push to main/master, warn the user if they request it\n'[39m +
            [32m'- CRITICAL: Always create NEW commits rather than amending, unless the user explicitly requests a git amend. When a pre-commit hook fails, the commit did NOT happen  — so --amend would modify the PREVIOUS commit, which may result in destroying work or losing previous changes. Instead, after hook failure, fix the issue, re-stage, and create a NEW commit\n'[39m +
            [32m'- When staging files, prefer adding specific files by name rather than using "git add -A" or "git add .", which can accidentally include sensitive files (.env, credentials) or large binaries\n'[39m +
            [32m'- NEVER commit changes unless the user explicitly asks you to. It is VERY IMPORTANT to only commit when explicitly asked, otherwise the user will feel that you are being too proactive\n'[39m +
            [32m'\n'[39m +
            [32m'1. You can call multiple tools in a single response. When multiple independent pieces of information are requested and all commands are likely to succeed, run multiple tool calls in parallel for optimal performance. run the following bash commands in parallel, each using the executeCommand tool:\n'[39m +
            [32m'  - Run a git status command to see all untracked files. IMPORTANT: Never use the -uall flag as it can cause memory issues on large repos.\n'[39m +
            [32m'  - Run a git diff command to see both staged and unstaged changes that will be committed.\n'[39m +
            [32m"  - Run a git log command to see recent commit messages, so that you can follow this repository's commit message style.\n"[39m +
            [32m'2. Analyze all staged changes (both previously staged and newly added) and draft a commit message:\n'[39m +
            [32m'  - Summarize the nature of the changes (eg. new feature, enhancement to an existing feature, bug fix, refactoring, test, docs, etc.). Ensure the message accurately reflects the changes and their purpose (i.e. "add" means a wholly new feature, "update" means an enhancement to an existing feature, "fix" means a bug fix, etc.).\n'[39m +
            [32m'  - Do not commit files that likely contain secrets (.env, credentials.json, etc). Warn the user if they specifically request to commit those files\n'[39m +
            [32m'  - Draft a concise (1-2 sentences) commit message that focuses on the "why" rather than the "what"\n'[39m +
            [32m'  - Ensure it accurately reflects the changes and their purpose\n'[39m +
